## §C Red-team checklist

1. `mark_failed` callers in other modules — checked: only `enqueue_research_run` actor calls it across src/. Old positional signature preserved (`mark_failed(run_id, error)` still works); new kwargs default to None.
2. error_json is freeform JSON — `_row_to_response` parses error_json into a dict for the API; new keys (`uploaded_documents_used`, `uploaded_documents_blocked`) don't break any consumer since they're added optionally.
3. POST /runs at runs.py:81 — when payload validation fails (21 ids), FastAPI returns 422 BEFORE entering the handler body. `_resolve_uploaded_documents` (which returns 400 on missing id) never runs.
4. The `actors.py` per-iteration `upload_counts` dict captures the post-sovereignty-filter `allowed_uploads` size — same semantics as the success-path INFO log.
5. `mark_failed` writes `error_json = json.dumps(error_payload, sort_keys=True)` — sort_keys keeps test diff-stable.
6. 5/5 new tests pass via the v6 actor's `.fn()` direct-invoke path with pre-inserted run row (per Codex brief iter-1 P2 caveat acknowledged).
7. No frontend-visible change; web/ TypeScript untouched.

 def cancel_research_run(run_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
     """Cancel an in-flight research run by run_id.

 def set_pipeline_meta(
     run_id: str,
     *,
     query_slug: str | None = None,
     manifest_run_id: str | None = None,
     artifact_dir: str | None = None,
     decision_id: str | None = None,
     path: str | None = None,
 ) -> None:
     """Set pipeline-A metadata after the actor learns the slug/dir.
 
     Independent of lifecycle transition so the actor can record meta as
     soon as pipeline-A starts, before the run completes.
     """
     conn = _connect(path)
     try:
         conn.execute(
             "UPDATE runs SET query_slug=COALESCE(?, query_slug), "
             "manifest_run_id=COALESCE(?, manifest_run_id), "
             "artifact_dir=COALESCE(?, artifact_dir), "
             "decision_id=COALESCE(?, decision_id) WHERE run_id=?",
             (query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, decision_id, run_id),
         )
         conn.commit()
     finally:
         conn.close()
 
 
 def mark_completed(
     run_id: str,
     result: dict[str, Any],
     *,
     pipeline_status: str = "success",
     cost_usd: float | None = None,
     path: str | None = None,
 ) -> None:
     """Transition in_progress → completed; set finished_at + result_json + pipeline_status + cost_usd."""
     conn = _connect(path)
     try:
         conn.execute(
             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='completed', finished_at=?, result_json=?, "
             "pipeline_status=?, cost_usd=? WHERE run_id=?",
             (_now_iso(), json.dumps(result, sort_keys=True), pipeline_status, cost_usd, run_id),
         )
         conn.commit()
     finally:
         conn.close()
 
 
 def mark_aborted(
     run_id: str,
     *,
     pipeline_status: str,
     abort_reason: str,
     cost_usd: float | None = None,
     path: str | None = None,
 ) -> None:
     """Pipeline ran to completion but hit a gate; lifecycle_status='completed', pipeline_status='abort_*'.
 
     Per CLAUDE.md §9.3, abort_* are pipeline verdicts (not errors). The run
     completed operationally; the pipeline-A logic chose to halt at a gate.
     """
     conn = _connect(path)
     try:
         conn.execute(
             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='completed', finished_at=?, "
             "pipeline_status=?, error_json=?, cost_usd=? WHERE run_id=?",
             (
                 _now_iso(),
                 pipeline_status,
                 json.dumps({"abort_reason": abort_reason}, sort_keys=True),
                 cost_usd,
                 run_id,
             ),
         )
         conn.commit()
     finally:
         conn.close()

 def _row_to_response(row: sqlite3.Row) -> RunStatusResponse:
     return RunStatusResponse(
         run_id=row["run_id"],
         template=row["template"],
         question=row["question"],
         lifecycle_status=row["lifecycle_status"],
         pipeline_status=row["pipeline_status"],
         queued_at=row["queued_at"],
         started_at=row["started_at"],
         finished_at=row["finished_at"],
         result_json=row["result_json"],
         error_json=row["error_json"],
         query_slug=row["query_slug"],
         manifest_run_id=row["manifest_run_id"],
         artifact_dir=row["artifact_dir"],
         cost_usd=row["cost_usd"],
         decision_id=row["decision_id"],
         cancel_requested=bool(row["cancel_requested"]),
     )
 
 
 def get_run(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> RunStatusResponse | None:
     """Return the run record or None if missing.
 
     Defensive against `OperationalError: no such table` so callers in stub
     mode (e.g. `tests/v6/test_actors.py` direct `.fn()` invocation without
     init_db) get None back, matching the actor's row-missing-stub-noop
     contract.
 
     I-arch-001a Codex iter-2 P2-002: if a known DB exists with the legacy
     schema, the first read-only `get_run` call would 500 on column-missing.
     The defensive catch below detects "no such column" and triggers a
     one-time migration via init_db before retrying.
     """
     conn = _connect(path)
     try:
         try:
             row = conn.execute(
                 f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs WHERE run_id=?",
                 (run_id,),
             ).fetchone()
         except sqlite3.OperationalError as exc:
             msg = str(exc).lower()
             # Narrow per Codex iter-1 P2-001: only the missing-table stub
             # path returns None; surface other operational errors (schema
             # corruption, migration faults) so they aren't masked as
             # missing-row.
             if "no such table" in msg:
                 return None
             # Codex iter-2 P2-002: legacy schema → migrate then retry once.
             if "no such column" in msg:
                 conn.close()
                 init_db(path)
                 conn = _connect(path)
                 row = conn.execute(
                     f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs WHERE run_id=?",
                     (run_id,),
                 ).fetchone()
             else:
                 raise
     finally:
         conn.close()
     if row is None:
         return None
     return _row_to_response(row)

     the run currently holding the session slot. At most one run is active
     once `insert_run_if_idle` gates all inserts; the `ORDER BY queued_at`
     is defensive (oldest first) for any pre-gate legacy rows.

+def _read_error_json(db_path: Path, run_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
+    import sqlite3
+
+    conn = sqlite3.connect(str(db_path))
+    try:
+        row = conn.execute(
+            "SELECT error_json FROM runs WHERE run_id=?", (run_id,)
+        ).fetchone()
+    finally:
+        conn.close()
+    assert row is not None and row[0]

+def _invoke_actor(*, run_id: str, allowed: list[dict], blocked_count: int, run_one_query_behavior):
+    """Run the v6 actor logic with a controlled mock of run_one_query.

+                pass

   5: - New columns: query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, pipeline_status,
   6:   cost_usd, decision_id (all nullable; backward-compatible)
   7: - New helpers: mark_failed, mark_aborted, set_pipeline_meta
   8: - get_run returns the full RunStatusResponse with new optional fields
   9: 
  10: I-rdy-011 (2026-05-16): cancellation support.
  11: - New column: cancel_requested (INTEGER 0/1).
  12: - request_cancel: queued → cancelled atomically (T1, instant); in_progress
  13:   → set the cancel flag (T2, cooperative — the worker observes it).
  14: - mark_in_progress is now a compare-and-swap (only transitions a queued,
  15:   not-cancel-requested row) so a queued cancel cannot be overwritten.
  16: - is_cancel_requested / mark_cancelled support the worker's cooperative
  17:   abort path.
  18: 
  19: I-rdy-013 (2026-05-16): 1-concurrent-session enforcement.
  20: - get_active_run: read-side helper — the run currently holding the session.
  21: - insert_run_if_idle: atomic check-and-insert (BEGIN IMMEDIATE) used by
  22:   POST /runs so a 2nd concurrent request cannot start a parallel session.
  23: - init_db serialized by `_INIT_LOCK`; `_connect` sets `busy_timeout`.
  24: 
  25: Default DB path: state/v6_runs.sqlite (gitignored). Override via env
  26: `POLARIS_V6_RUN_DB`. WAL mode enabled.
  27: """
  28: 
  29: from __future__ import annotations
  30: 
  31: import json
  32: import os
  33: import sqlite3
  34: import threading
  35: from datetime import datetime, timezone
  36: from typing import Any
  37: 
  38: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_status import RunStatusResponse
  39: 
  40: DEFAULT_DB_PATH = "state/v6_runs.sqlite"
  41: ENV_DB_PATH = "POLARIS_V6_RUN_DB"
  42: 
  43: # Lifecycle states from which a run can no longer transition. Public so the
  44: # /runs/{id}/cancel endpoint shares one definition of "terminal".
  45: TERMINAL_STATUSES = ("completed", "failed", "cancelled")
  46: 
  47: # Columns selected by get_run (single source of truth for both the
  48: # first-attempt and post-migration-retry queries).
  49: _RUN_COLUMNS = (
  50:     "run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, pipeline_status, "
  51:     "queued_at, started_at, finished_at, result_json, error_json, "
  52:     "query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, cost_usd, decision_id, "
  53:     "cancel_requested"
  54: )
  55: 
  56: # I-rdy-013: lifecycle states that count as an active research session. A run
  57: # in one of these blocks a new POST /runs (1-concurrent-session constraint).
  58: # `completed`, `cancelled`, `failed` are terminal and free the session slot.
  59: _ACTIVE_STATUSES = ("queued", "in_progress")
  60: 
  61: # I-rdy-013: serializes init_db across in-process threads so two concurrent
  62: # first requests cannot collide inside `PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL` or the schema
  63: # migration and raise sqlite3.OperationalError before the atomic gate runs.
  64: _INIT_LOCK = threading.Lock()
  65: 
  66: 
  67: def _resolve_path(path: str | None) -> str:
  68:     if path is not None:
  69:         return path
  70:     return os.environ.get(ENV_DB_PATH, DEFAULT_DB_PATH)
  71: 
  72: 
  73: def _now_iso() -> str:
  74:     return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
  75: 
  76: 
  77: def _connect(path: str | None = None) -> sqlite3.Connection:
  78:     resolved = _resolve_path(path)
  79:     parent = os.path.dirname(resolved)
  80:     if parent:
  81:         os.makedirs(parent, exist_ok=True)
  82:     conn = sqlite3.connect(resolved)
  83:     conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
  84:     # I-rdy-013: a concurrent writer waits up to 5s for the write lock
  85:     # instead of raising SQLITE_BUSY immediately (the issue's "no crash").
  86:     conn.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000")
  87:     return conn
  88: 
  89: 
  90: def _migrate_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
  91:     """Idempotent additive migration. Safe to call on every init_db.
  92: 
  93:     1. Create base table if absent.
  94:     2. If legacy `status` column exists and `lifecycle_status` doesn't,
  95:        RENAME COLUMN to preserve values (SQLite 3.25+, Python 3.11 ships
  96:        SQLite 3.34+).
  97:     3. ADD COLUMN for each I-arch-001a / I-rdy-011 field if missing.
  98:     4. CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS for query lookups.
  99:     """
 100:     conn.execute(
 101:         """
 102:         CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS runs (
 103:             run_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
 104:             template TEXT NOT NULL,
 105:             question TEXT NOT NULL,
 106:             lifecycle_status TEXT NOT NULL,
 107:             queued_at TEXT NOT NULL,
 108:             started_at TEXT,
 109:             finished_at TEXT,
 110:             result_json TEXT,
 111:             error_json TEXT
 112:         )
 113:         """
 114:     )
 115:     cols = {row[1] for row in conn.execute("PRAGMA table_info(runs)").fetchall()}
 116:     if "status" in cols and "lifecycle_status" not in cols:
 117:         conn.execute("ALTER TABLE runs RENAME COLUMN status TO lifecycle_status")
 118:         cols.discard("status")
 119:         cols.add("lifecycle_status")
 120:     for col_name, col_type in {
 121:         "query_slug": "TEXT",
 122:         "manifest_run_id": "TEXT",
 123:         "artifact_dir": "TEXT",
 124:         "pipeline_status": "TEXT",
 125:         "cost_usd": "REAL",
 126:         "decision_id": "TEXT",
 127:         "cancel_requested": "INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0",
 128:     }.items():
 129:         if col_name not in cols:
 130:             conn.execute(f"ALTER TABLE runs ADD COLUMN {col_name} {col_type}")
 131:     conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_runs_query_slug ON runs(query_slug)")
 132:     conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_runs_manifest_run_id ON runs(manifest_run_id)")
 133: 
 134: 
 135: def init_db(path: str | None = None) -> None:
 136:     """Create the runs table if absent, run migrations. Idempotent.
 137: 
 138:     I-rdy-013: serialized by `_INIT_LOCK` so two concurrent first requests
 139:     (FastAPI worker threads, one process) cannot collide inside
 140:     `PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL` or the schema migration and raise
 141:     sqlite3.OperationalError before the atomic gate is reached.
 142:     """
 143:     with _INIT_LOCK:
 144:         conn = _connect(path)
 145:         try:
 146:             conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
 147:             _migrate_schema(conn)
 148:             conn.commit()
 149:         finally:
 150:             conn.close()
 151: 
 152: 
 153: def insert_run(run_id: str, template: str, question: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> None:
 154:     """Insert a new row with lifecycle_status='queued'. Raises IntegrityError on duplicate.
 155: 
 156:     Unconditional primitive — does NOT enforce the 1-concurrent-session
 157:     constraint. POST /runs uses `insert_run_if_idle`; this remains for test
 158:     fixtures and any caller that deliberately wants an unconditional insert.
 159:     """
 160:     init_db(path)
 161:     conn = _connect(path)
 162:     try:
 163:         conn.execute(
 164:             "INSERT INTO runs (run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, queued_at) "
 165:             "VALUES (?, ?, ?, 'queued', ?)",
 166:             (run_id, template, question, _now_iso()),
 167:         )
 168:         conn.commit()
 169:     finally:
 170:         conn.close()
 171: 
 172: 
 173: def insert_run_if_idle(
 174:     run_id: str, template: str, question: str, *, path: str | None = None
 175: ) -> RunStatusResponse | None:
 176:     """Atomically insert a new queued run IFF no run is currently active.
 177: 
 178:     I-rdy-013 (1-concurrent-session enforcement): the check-for-active and
 179:     the INSERT run inside one `BEGIN IMMEDIATE` transaction, so two
 180:     concurrent POST /runs cannot both pass the check. `BEGIN IMMEDIATE`
 181:     takes the write lock up-front; the 2nd writer blocks on it (up to the
 182:     `busy_timeout`) until the 1st commits, then sees the inserted row.
 183: 
 184:     Returns None when the run was inserted; returns the blocking active
 185:     RunStatusResponse when rejected (caller raises HTTP 409).
 186:     """
 187:     init_db(path)
 188:     placeholders = ", ".join("?" for _ in _ACTIVE_STATUSES)
 189:     conn = _connect(path)
 190:     conn.isolation_level = None  # manual transaction control
 191:     try:
 192:         conn.execute("BEGIN IMMEDIATE")
 193:         row = conn.execute(
 194:             f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs "
 195:             f"WHERE lifecycle_status IN ({placeholders}) "
 196:             "ORDER BY queued_at LIMIT 1",
 197:             _ACTIVE_STATUSES,
 198:         ).fetchone()
 199:         if row is not None:
 200:             conn.execute("ROLLBACK")
 201:             return _row_to_response(row)
 202:         conn.execute(
 203:             "INSERT INTO runs (run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, queued_at) "
 204:             "VALUES (?, ?, ?, 'queued', ?)",
 205:             (run_id, template, question, _now_iso()),
 206:         )
 207:         conn.execute("COMMIT")
 208:         return None
 209:     finally:
 210:         conn.close()
 211: 
 212: 
 213: def mark_in_progress(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> bool:
 214:     """Transition queued → in_progress IFF the run is not cancel-requested.
 215: 
 216:     I-rdy-011: compare-and-swap. The `WHERE lifecycle_status='queued' AND
 217:     cancel_requested=0` guard means a queued cancel that already flipped the
 218:     row to 'cancelled' cannot be overwritten by a worker picking the run up.
 219: 
 220:     Returns True iff the row transitioned; False means the run was cancelled
 221:     (or already past 'queued') and the caller must not run the pipeline.
 222:     """
 223:     conn = _connect(path)
 224:     try:
 225:         cur = conn.execute(
 226:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='in_progress', started_at=? "
 227:             "WHERE run_id=? AND lifecycle_status='queued' AND cancel_requested=0",
 228:             (_now_iso(), run_id),
 229:         )
 230:         conn.commit()
 231:         return cur.rowcount > 0
 232:     finally:
 233:         conn.close()
 234: 
 235: 
 236: def request_cancel(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> str | None:
 237:     """Request cancellation of a run (I-rdy-011).
 238: 
 239:     - queued run → atomically transitioned to terminal 'cancelled' (T1,
 240:       instant — the worker's mark_in_progress CAS will then no-op).
 241:     - in_progress run → cancel_requested flag set; lifecycle stays
 242:       'in_progress' until the worker observes the flag at a pipeline stage
 243:       boundary and calls mark_cancelled (T2, cooperative).
 244: 
 245:     Returns the resulting lifecycle_status ('cancelled' or 'in_progress'),
 246:     or None if the run does not exist or is already terminal.
 247:     """
 248:     conn = _connect(path)
 249:     try:
 250:         # T1: queued → cancelled, atomically.
 251:         cur = conn.execute(
 252:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='cancelled', cancel_requested=1, "
 253:             "finished_at=? WHERE run_id=? AND lifecycle_status='queued'",
 254:             (_now_iso(), run_id),
 255:         )
 256:         if cur.rowcount > 0:
 257:             conn.commit()
 258:             return "cancelled"
 259:         # T2: in_progress → set the flag for the worker to observe.
 260:         cur = conn.execute(
 261:             "UPDATE runs SET cancel_requested=1 "
 262:             "WHERE run_id=? AND lifecycle_status='in_progress'",
 263:             (run_id,),
 264:         )
 265:         conn.commit()
 266:         return "in_progress" if cur.rowcount > 0 else None
 267:     finally:
 268:         conn.close()
 269: 
 270: 
 271: def is_cancel_requested(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> bool:
 272:     """True iff a cancellation has been requested for the run.
 273: 
 274:     Best-effort: a missing run / missing table returns False.
 275:     """
 276:     conn = _connect(path)
 277:     try:
 278:         try:
 279:             row = conn.execute(
 280:                 "SELECT cancel_requested FROM runs WHERE run_id=?", (run_id,)
 281:             ).fetchone()
 282:         except sqlite3.OperationalError:
 283:             return False
 284:         return bool(row["cancel_requested"]) if row is not None else False
 285:     finally:
 286:         conn.close()
 287: 
 288: 
 289: def mark_cancelled(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> None:
 290:     """Terminal transition → lifecycle_status='cancelled' + finished_at.
 291: 
 292:     Used by the worker when it observes cancel_requested at a pipeline
 293:     stage boundary (cooperative T2 abort), and as the actor's mapping for a
 294:     pipeline-A manifest with status 'cancelled'.
 295:     """
 296:     conn = _connect(path)
 297:     try:
 298:         conn.execute(
 299:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='cancelled', cancel_requested=1, "
 300:             "finished_at=? WHERE run_id=?",
 301:             (_now_iso(), run_id),
 302:         )
 303:         conn.commit()
 304:     finally:
 305:         conn.close()
 306: 
 307: 
 308: def set_pipeline_meta(
 309:     run_id: str,
 310:     *,
 311:     query_slug: str | None = None,
 312:     manifest_run_id: str | None = None,
 313:     artifact_dir: str | None = None,
 314:     decision_id: str | None = None,
 315:     path: str | None = None,
 316: ) -> None:
 317:     """Set pipeline-A metadata after the actor learns the slug/dir.
 318: 
 319:     Independent of lifecycle transition so the actor can record meta as
 320:     soon as pipeline-A starts, before the run completes.
 321:     """
 322:     conn = _connect(path)
 323:     try:
 324:         conn.execute(
 325:             "UPDATE runs SET query_slug=COALESCE(?, query_slug), "
 326:             "manifest_run_id=COALESCE(?, manifest_run_id), "
 327:             "artifact_dir=COALESCE(?, artifact_dir), "
 328:             "decision_id=COALESCE(?, decision_id) WHERE run_id=?",
 329:             (query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, decision_id, run_id),
 330:         )
 331:         conn.commit()
 332:     finally:
 333:         conn.close()
 334: 
 335: 
 336: def mark_completed(
 337:     run_id: str,
 338:     result: dict[str, Any],
 339:     *,
 340:     pipeline_status: str = "success",
 341:     cost_usd: float | None = None,
 342:     path: str | None = None,
 343: ) -> None:
 344:     """Transition in_progress → completed; set finished_at + result_json + pipeline_status + cost_usd."""
 345:     conn = _connect(path)
 346:     try:
 347:         conn.execute(
 348:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='completed', finished_at=?, result_json=?, "
 349:             "pipeline_status=?, cost_usd=? WHERE run_id=?",
 350:             (_now_iso(), json.dumps(result, sort_keys=True), pipeline_status, cost_usd, run_id),
 351:         )
 352:         conn.commit()
 353:     finally:
 354:         conn.close()

 356: 
 357: def mark_aborted(
 358:     run_id: str,
 359:     *,
 360:     pipeline_status: str,
 361:     abort_reason: str,
 362:     cost_usd: float | None = None,
 363:     path: str | None = None,
 364: ) -> None:
 365:     """Pipeline ran to completion but hit a gate; lifecycle_status='completed', pipeline_status='abort_*'.
 366: 
 367:     Per CLAUDE.md §9.3, abort_* are pipeline verdicts (not errors). The run
 368:     completed operationally; the pipeline-A logic chose to halt at a gate.
 369:     """
 370:     conn = _connect(path)

 388: def mark_failed(
 389:     run_id: str,
 390:     error: str,
 391:     *,
 392:     path: str | None = None,
 393:     uploaded_documents_used: int | None = None,
 394:     uploaded_documents_blocked: int | None = None,
 395: ) -> None:
 396:     """Operational failure (exception, missing manifest, unknown status, etc).
 397: 
 398:     Distinct from mark_aborted: failures are unplanned (exception or invariant
 399:     violation); aborts are planned (pipeline_status='abort_*' written by
 400:     pipeline-A at a gate).
 401: 
 402:     I-cd-018 (#628): optional `uploaded_documents_used` +
 403:     `uploaded_documents_blocked` flow into `error_json` so the error-path
 404:     observability mirrors the success-path INFO log (actors.py:146-151).
 405:     Keys are present in error_json only when caller passes them.
 406:     """
 407:     error_payload: dict[str, object] = {"error": error}
 408:     if uploaded_documents_used is not None:
 409:         error_payload["uploaded_documents_used"] = uploaded_documents_used
 410:     if uploaded_documents_blocked is not None:
 411:         error_payload["uploaded_documents_blocked"] = uploaded_documents_blocked
 412:     conn = _connect(path)
 413:     try:
 414:         conn.execute(
 415:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='failed', finished_at=?, "
 416:             "pipeline_status='error_unexpected', error_json=? WHERE run_id=?",
 417:             (_now_iso(), json.dumps(error_payload, sort_keys=True), run_id),
 418:         )
 419:         conn.commit()
 420:     finally:
 421:         conn.close()

 445: def get_run(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> RunStatusResponse | None:
 446:     """Return the run record or None if missing.
 447: 
 448:     Defensive against `OperationalError: no such table` so callers in stub
 449:     mode (e.g. `tests/v6/test_actors.py` direct `.fn()` invocation without
 450:     init_db) get None back, matching the actor's row-missing-stub-noop
 451:     contract.
 452: 
 453:     I-arch-001a Codex iter-2 P2-002: if a known DB exists with the legacy
 454:     schema, the first read-only `get_run` call would 500 on column-missing.
 455:     The defensive catch below detects "no such column" and triggers a
 456:     one-time migration via init_db before retrying.
 457:     """
 458:     conn = _connect(path)
 459:     try:
 460:         try:
 461:             row = conn.execute(
 462:                 f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs WHERE run_id=?",
 463:                 (run_id,),
 464:             ).fetchone()
 465:         except sqlite3.OperationalError as exc:
 466:             msg = str(exc).lower()
 467:             # Narrow per Codex iter-1 P2-001: only the missing-table stub
 468:             # path returns None; surface other operational errors (schema
 469:             # corruption, migration faults) so they aren't masked as
 470:             # missing-row.

   1: """Runs router — POST /runs, GET /runs/{id}, POST /runs/{id}/cancel.
   2: 
   3: I-phase0-005 (Codex APPROVE iter 4): persist runs to SQLite via
   4: polaris_v6.queue.run_store and enqueue the Dramatiq actor on POST.
   5: Replaces the previous in-memory `_run_table` dict.
   6: 
   7: I-rdy-010 (#506): POST /runs resolves uploaded `document_ids` to content
   8: BEFORE inserting/enqueuing the run, so a missing or unparsed upload fails
   9: loud here rather than leaving a queued orphan run. The resolved content is
  10: embedded in the actor message because the Dramatiq worker is a separate
  11: process and cannot read the API process's in-memory upload table.
  12: 
  13: I-rdy-011 (#507): POST /runs/{id}/cancel — a queued run cancels instantly;
  14: an in-progress run records the cancel request (the worker observes it at
  15: the next pipeline stage boundary). Already-terminal runs are an idempotent
  16: no-op.
  17: 
  18: I-rdy-013 (#509): POST /runs enforces the 1-concurrent-session constraint
  19: via `run_store.insert_run_if_idle` — a 2nd concurrent request is cleanly
  20: rejected with HTTP 409 (never enqueued) and a structured detail the
  21: frontend renders as a link to the active run.
  22: """
  23: 
  24: from __future__ import annotations
  25: 
  26: import sqlite3
  27: import uuid
  28: 
  29: from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
  30: 
  31: from polaris_v6.api.upload import chunk_text, get_upload_record
  32: from polaris_v6.queue import run_store
  33: from polaris_v6.queue.actors import enqueue_research_run
  34: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_request import RunRequest
  35: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_status import RunStatusResponse
  36: 
  37: router = APIRouter(prefix="/runs", tags=["runs"])

  39: 
  40: def _resolve_uploaded_documents(document_ids: list[str]) -> list[dict]:
  41:     """Resolve uploaded document_ids → content for actor-message embedding.
  42: 
  43:     Returns one dict per id: `{document_id, classification, filename,
  44:     chunks}`. `chunks` is `chunk_text(record.content)` — the full document
  45:     re-chunked (and capped), NOT the 3-chunk `chunk_preview`.
  46: 
  47:     Fails loud (HTTP 400) per LAW II on:
  48:       * a document_id with no upload record;
  49:       * an upload that yields no extractable text (e.g. an unparsed
  50:         pdf/docx) — a silent zero-evidence run would mislead the operator.
  51:     """
  52:     resolved: list[dict] = []
  53:     for document_id in document_ids:
  54:         record = get_upload_record(document_id)
  55:         if record is None:
  56:             raise HTTPException(
  57:                 status_code=400,
  58:                 detail=f"uploaded document {document_id!r} not found",
  59:             )
  60:         chunks = chunk_text(record.content)
  61:         if not chunks:
  62:             raise HTTPException(
  63:                 status_code=400,
  64:                 detail=(
  65:                     f"uploaded document {document_id!r} ({record.filename}) "
  66:                     "has no extractable text — pdf/docx parsing is not yet "
  67:                     "available; upload a .md or .txt document to ground a run."
  68:                 ),
  69:             )
  70:         resolved.append(
  71:             {
  72:                 "document_id": document_id,
  73:                 "classification": record.classification,
  74:                 "filename": record.filename,
  75:                 "chunks": chunks,
  76:             }
  77:         )
  78:     return resolved
  79: 
  80: 
  81: @router.post("", response_model=RunStatusResponse, status_code=202)
  82: def create_run(payload: RunRequest) -> RunStatusResponse:
  83:     # I-rdy-010: resolve uploads BEFORE insert_run/enqueue so a bad
  84:     # document_id fails loud here instead of orphaning a queued run.
  85:     uploaded_documents = _resolve_uploaded_documents(payload.document_ids)
  86: 
  87:     run_id = uuid.uuid4().hex
  88:     try:
  89:         # I-rdy-013: atomic 1-concurrent-session gate. Returns the blocking
  90:         # active run when rejected, None when this run was inserted.
  91:         active = run_store.insert_run_if_idle(
  92:             run_id, payload.template, payload.question
  93:         )
  94:     except sqlite3.IntegrityError as exc:
  95:         # uuid4 collision is theoretically impossible but defensive
  96:         raise HTTPException(status_code=409, detail=f"run {run_id!r} already exists") from exc
  97:     except RuntimeError as exc:
  98:         # init_db permission-denied or similar
  99:         raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail=str(exc)) from exc
 100: 
 101:     if active is not None:
 102:         # I-rdy-013: 1-concurrent-session constraint — a research run is
 103:         # already queued or in progress. Reject cleanly; the rejected run is
 104:         # never enqueued (insert_run_if_idle rolled back — no row to clean
 105:         # up). The structured `detail` lets the frontend render a specific
 106:         # UX with a link to the active run.
 107:         raise HTTPException(
 108:             status_code=409,
 109:             detail={
 110:                 "code": "concurrent_run_active",
 111:                 "active_run_id": active.run_id,
 112:                 "active_status": active.lifecycle_status,
 113:                 "message": (
 114:                     "POLARIS runs one research session at a time. "
 115:                     f"Run {active.run_id[:8]} is currently {active.lifecycle_status}. "
 116:                     "Wait for it to finish before starting a new run."
 117:                 ),
 118:             },
 119:         )
 120: 
 121:     # The actor message carries the resolved upload content (the worker is
 122:     # a separate process — it cannot read the API process's upload table).
 123:     actor_payload = payload.model_dump()
 124:     actor_payload["uploaded_documents"] = uploaded_documents
 125:     try:
 126:         enqueue_research_run.send(run_id, actor_payload)
 127:     except Exception as exc:
 128:         # I-rdy-013 (Codex diff P1-001): the queued row is already committed.
 129:         # If enqueue fails it would never run yet would permanently hold the
 130:         # single-session slot. Mark it failed (terminal → frees the slot),
 131:         # then surface 503.
 132:         run_store.mark_failed(run_id, f"enqueue failed: {exc}")
 133:         raise HTTPException(
 134:             status_code=503,
 135:             detail=f"failed to enqueue run {run_id!r}: {exc}",
 136:         ) from exc
 137: 
 138:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 139:     if record is None:  # pragma: no cover — insert just succeeded
 140:         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="run row vanished after insert")
 141:     return record
 142: 
 143: 
 144: @router.get("/{run_id}", response_model=RunStatusResponse)
 145: def get_run(run_id: str) -> RunStatusResponse:
 146:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 147:     if record is None:
 148:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"run {run_id!r} not found")
 149:     return record
 150: 
 151: 
 152: @router.post("/{run_id}/cancel", response_model=RunStatusResponse)
 153: def cancel_run(run_id: str) -> RunStatusResponse:
 154:     """Request cancellation of a run (I-rdy-011 / #507).
 155: 
 156:     - Unknown run → 404.
 157:     - Already terminal (completed / failed / cancelled) → idempotent no-op,
 158:       returns the current record (200).
 159:     - queued → cancelled instantly; in_progress → cancel requested, the
 160:       worker aborts cooperatively at the next pipeline stage boundary.
 161:     """
 162:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 163:     if record is None:
 164:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"run {run_id!r} not found")
 165:     if record.lifecycle_status in run_store.TERMINAL_STATUSES:
 166:         return record  # idempotent — nothing to cancel
 167: 
 168:     run_store.request_cancel(run_id)
 169: 
 170:     updated = run_store.get_run(run_id)
 171:     if updated is None:  # pragma: no cover — the row existed a line ago
 172:         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="run row vanished after cancel")
 173:     return updated

 succeeded in 929ms:
   1: """Uploaded-document grounding for the v6 research pipeline (I-rdy-010 / #506).
   2: 
   3: The v6 worker actor resolves uploaded ``document_ids`` to content, then this
   4: module does two things:
   5: 
   6: 1. ``partition_uploads_by_sovereignty`` — splits resolved uploads into
   7:    egress-allowed vs egress-blocked via the sovereignty router. The pipeline
   8:    generator is an external LLM call, so only ``PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC`` documents
   9:    may become evidence; ``CLIENT`` / ``CAN_REAL`` / ``PRIVATE`` / ``UNKNOWN``
  10:    are ``EXTERNAL_LEAK_FORBIDDEN`` and never reach the generator.
  11: 2. ``build_upload_evidence_rows`` — turns sovereignty-cleared documents into
  12:    the pipeline-A evidence dict-row shape (matching the V30-P2 contract rows
  13:    at ``scripts/run_honest_sweep_r3.py:2044-2059``), so uploaded-document
  14:    evidence is prepended onto ``evidence_for_gen`` and flows into the report
  15:    bibliography + ``evidence_pool.json``.
  16: 
  17: Per CLAUDE.md LAW II: a forbidden classification reaching
  18: ``build_upload_evidence_rows`` raises rather than silently passing — the
  19: actor-stage sovereignty filter is the gate, and this re-check is
  20: belt-and-suspenders.
  21: """
  22: 
  23: from __future__ import annotations
  24: 
  25: from polaris_graph.sovereignty.router import filter_for_external_egress
  26: 
  27: # Only PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC uploads may become external-generator evidence;
  28: # every other classification is EXTERNAL_LEAK_FORBIDDEN.
  29: EGRESS_SAFE_CLASSIFICATION = "PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC"
  30: 
  31: 
  32: class UploadSovereigntyError(RuntimeError):
  33:     """Raised when a non-egress-safe uploaded document reaches evidence-row
  34:     construction. A forbidden document here is a bug — the actor-stage
  35:     sovereignty filter should have blocked it — never a silent pass."""
  36: 
  37: 
  38: def partition_uploads_by_sovereignty(
  39:     uploaded_documents: list[dict],
  40: ) -> tuple[list[dict], list[dict]]:
  41:     """Split uploaded documents into (egress-allowed, egress-blocked).
  42: 
  43:     Each document is a dict carrying a ``classification`` key. Delegates to
  44:     the sovereignty router (``filter_for_external_egress``, non-strict) so
  45:     the EXTERNAL_LEAK_FORBIDDEN policy is enforced in exactly one place.
  46:     """
  47:     decision = filter_for_external_egress(uploaded_documents, strict=False)
  48:     return list(decision.allowed), list(decision.blocked)
  49: 
  50: 
  51: def build_upload_evidence_rows(uploaded_documents: list[dict]) -> list[dict]:
  52:     """Build pipeline-A evidence dict rows from sovereignty-cleared uploads.
  53: 
  54:     Args:
  55:         uploaded_documents: list of ``{document_id, classification,
  56:             filename, chunks}`` — expected to be the *allowed* partition
  57:             from ``partition_uploads_by_sovereignty``.
  58: 
  59:     Returns:
  60:         One evidence dict row per non-empty chunk, shaped like the V30-P2
  61:         contract rows so the generator + ``evidence_pool`` consume them.
  62: 
  63:     Raises:
  64:         UploadSovereigntyError: if any document is not PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC.
  65:     """
  66:     rows: list[dict] = []
  67:     for doc in uploaded_documents:
  68:         classification = doc.get("classification")
  69:         if classification != EGRESS_SAFE_CLASSIFICATION:
  70:             raise UploadSovereigntyError(
  71:                 f"uploaded document {doc.get('document_id')!r} has "
  72:                 f"classification {classification!r}; only "
  73:                 f"{EGRESS_SAFE_CLASSIFICATION} may become external-generator "
  74:                 "evidence — the actor-stage sovereignty filter should have "
  75:                 "blocked this document."
  76:             )
  77:         document_id = doc["document_id"]
  78:         filename = doc.get("filename") or "uploaded document"
  79:         for chunk_index, chunk in enumerate(doc.get("chunks") or []):
  80:             text = (chunk or "").strip()
  81:             if not text:
  82:                 continue
  83:             rows.append(
  84:                 {
  85:                     "evidence_id": f"ev_upload_{document_id}_{chunk_index}",
  86:                     "statement": text,
  87:                     "direct_quote": text,
  88:                     "source_url": f"upload://{document_id}",
  89:                     "title": filename,
  90:                     "authors": [],
  91:                     "journal": "",
  92:                     "year": None,
  93:                     "doi": "",
  94:                     "pmid": "",
  95:                     "tier": "T2",
  96:                     "uploaded_document": True,
  97:                 }
  98:             )
  99:     return rows

   1: """POST /upload — F3b drag-drop document upload endpoint.
   2: 
   3: Per docs/carney_delivery_plan_v6_2.md F3b, the user can upload PDFs /
   4: docx / md / txt to seed a research run. Phase 0 ships the contract:
   5: returns a document_id + parse_status; Phase 1 wires actual parsing +
   6: chunking + sovereignty router (CAN_REAL data must stay on Canadian
   7: infra).
   8: 
   9: Per CLAUDE.md security posture: file content classification
  10: (PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC | CAN_REAL | PRIVATE | CLIENT | UNKNOWN) is set by
  11: the caller; default is UNKNOWN and triggers conservative routing.
  12: 
  13: I-rdy-010 (#506): `get_upload_record` + `chunk_text` let POST /runs
  14: resolve uploaded document_ids to content at run-creation time. The
  15: upload table is an in-process dict — the Dramatiq worker is a separate
  16: process and cannot read it — so /runs (which runs in the API process)
  17: resolves the content and embeds it in the actor message.
  18: """
  19: 
  20: from __future__ import annotations
  21: 
  22: import hashlib
  23: import html as _html
  24: import uuid
  25: from typing import Literal
  26: 
  27: from fastapi import APIRouter, Form, HTTPException, UploadFile
  28: from pydantic import BaseModel
  29: 
  30: router = APIRouter(prefix="/upload", tags=["upload"])
  31: 
  32: DataClassification = Literal[
  33:     "PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC",
  34:     "CAN_REAL",
  35:     "PRIVATE",
  36:     "CLIENT",
  37:     "UNKNOWN",
  38: ]
  39: 
  40: ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS = {".pdf", ".docx", ".md", ".txt"}
  41: MAX_BYTES = 50 * 1024 * 1024  # 50 MB per upload (I-f3-005 frontend dropzone)
  42: 
  43: # I-rdy-010 (#506): grounding-chunk parameters. CHUNK_SIZE matches the
  44: # upload-endpoint preview chunking; MAX_GROUNDING_CHUNKS bounds how much
  45: # uploaded text is embedded into a Dramatiq actor message — a .md/.txt
  46: # upload can be up to MAX_BYTES, so the full document is NOT embedded.
  47: CHUNK_SIZE = 280
  48: MAX_GROUNDING_CHUNKS = 40
  49: 
  50: 
  51: class UploadResponse(BaseModel):
  52:     document_id: str
  53:     filename: str
  54:     bytes: int
  55:     sha256: str
  56:     classification: DataClassification
  57:     parse_status: Literal["queued", "completed", "failed"]
  58:     chunk_preview: list[str]
  59:     content: str = ""
  60:     html: str = ""
  61: 
  62: 
  63: _UPLOAD_TABLE: dict[str, UploadResponse] = {}
  64: 
  65: 
  66: def chunk_text(
  67:     text: str,
  68:     *,
  69:     size: int = CHUNK_SIZE,
  70:     max_chunks: int = MAX_GROUNDING_CHUNKS,
  71: ) -> list[str]:
  72:     """Split text into fixed-size chunks, capped at ``max_chunks``.
  73: 
  74:     The cap bounds the embedded actor-message payload (I-rdy-010) — an
  75:     uploaded .md/.txt document can be up to ``MAX_BYTES``, so only the
  76:     leading ``max_chunks`` are used to ground a run.
  77:     """
  78:     text = text.strip()
  79:     if not text:
  80:         return []
  81:     chunks = [text[i : i + size] for i in range(0, len(text), size)]
  82:     return chunks[:max_chunks]
  83: 
  84: 
  85: def get_upload_record(document_id: str) -> UploadResponse | None:
  86:     """Look up an uploaded document by id, or None if absent.
  87: 
  88:     Used by POST /runs (I-rdy-010) to resolve document_ids → content at
  89:     run-creation time, in the API process that owns ``_UPLOAD_TABLE``.
  90:     """
  91:     return _UPLOAD_TABLE.get(document_id)
  92: 
  93: 
  94: @router.post("", response_model=UploadResponse, status_code=201)
  95: async def upload_document(
  96:     file: UploadFile,
  97:     classification: DataClassification = Form("UNKNOWN"),
  98: ) -> UploadResponse:
  99:     if file.filename is None:
 100:         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="filename required")
 101: 
 102:     ext = "." + file.filename.rsplit(".", 1)[-1].lower() if "." in file.filename else ""
 103:     if ext not in ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS:
 104:         raise HTTPException(
 105:             status_code=415,
 106:             detail=f"Unsupported extension {ext!r}. Allowed: {sorted(ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS)}",
 107:         )
 108: 
 109:     content = await file.read()
 110:     if len(content) > MAX_BYTES:
 111:         raise HTTPException(
 112:             status_code=413,
 113:             detail=f"File exceeds {MAX_BYTES // (1024 * 1024)} MB limit",
 114:         )
 115:     if len(content) == 0:
 116:         raise HTTPException(status_code=422, detail="empty file")
 117: 
 118:     sha = hashlib.sha256(content).hexdigest()
 119:     document_id = uuid.uuid4().hex
 120: 
 121:     if ext in {".md", ".txt"}:
 122:         try:
 123:             text = content.decode("utf-8", errors="replace")
 124:         except Exception:
 125:             text = ""
 126:         chunks = [text[i : i + 280] for i in range(0, min(len(text), 840), 280) if text]
 127:         preview_text = text
 128:         preview_html = f"<pre>{_html.escape(text)}</pre>" if text else ""
 129:     else:
 130:         chunks = []
 131:         preview_text = ""
 132:         preview_html = ""
 133: 
 134:     response = UploadResponse(
 135:         document_id=document_id,
 136:         filename=file.filename,
 137:         bytes=len(content),
 138:         sha256=sha,
 139:         classification=classification,
 140:         parse_status="completed" if chunks else "queued",
 141:         chunk_preview=chunks[:3],
 142:         content=preview_text,
 143:         html=preview_html,
 144:     )
 145:     _UPLOAD_TABLE[document_id] = response
 146:     return response
 147: 
 148: 
 149: @router.get("/{document_id}", response_model=UploadResponse)
 150: def get_upload(document_id: str) -> UploadResponse:
 151:     record = _UPLOAD_TABLE.get(document_id)
 152:     if record is None:
 153:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"document {document_id!r} not found")
 154:     return record

codex
I don’t see a P1-class break in the code paths so far. One boundary I’m still checking is whether the new schema constraint and kwargs remain compatible with the installed dependency versions and the existing v6 tests.

import json, os, sqlite3
from pathlib import Path
from unittest.mock import patch
from polaris_v6.queue import run_store, actors

base = Path('codex_review_tmp')
db = base / 'manual_actor.sqlite'
out = base / 'manual_actor_out'
os.environ[run_store.ENV_DB_PATH] = str(db)
os.environ['POLARIS_V6_OUTPUT_ROOT'] = str(out)
run_store.init_db(str(db))

def read_error(run_id):
    conn = sqlite3.connect(str(db))
    try:
        row = conn.execute('SELECT error_json FROM runs WHERE run_id=?', (run_id,)).fetchone()
    finally:
        conn.close()
    return json.loads(row[0])

def invoke(run_id, allowed, blocked_count, behavior):
    run_store.insert_run(run_id, 'clinical', 'test question?', path=str(db))
    payload = {'template': 'clinical', 'question': 'test question?', 'uploaded_documents': allowed}
    with patch('polaris_v6.adapters.upload_evidence.partition_uploads_by_sovereignty', return_value=(allowed, [{'document_id': f'blocked_{i}'} for i in range(blocked_count)])):
        with patch('scripts.run_honest_sweep_r3.run_one_query', side_effect=behavior):
            try:
                actors.enqueue_research_run.fn(run_id, payload)
            except RuntimeError:
                pass

def raises(*args, **kwargs):
    raise RuntimeError('boom')
invoke('manual_exc', [{'document_id':'d1','classification':'PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC','chunks':[]}], 2, raises)
print('exc', read_error('manual_exc'))

def no_manifest(q, artifact_dir_root):
    return {'run_id': q.get('external_run_id'), 'cost_usd': 0.0}
invoke('manual_missing', [{'document_id':'d1','classification':'PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC','chunks':[]},{'document_id':'d2','classification':'PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC','chunks':[]}], 0, no_manifest)
print('missing', read_error('manual_missing'))

def bad_manifest(q, artifact_dir_root):
    Path(artifact_dir_root).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    (Path(artifact_dir_root) / 'manifest.json').write_text('{not valid json', encoding='utf-8')
    return {'run_id': q.get('external_run_id'), 'cost_usd': 0.0}

print('invalid', read_error('manual_invalid'))

   1: """Test-level setup for tests/v6/.
   2: 
   3: Closes cycle-4 audit P1.1 (outputs/audits/continuous/97b9c1f_audit.md):
   4: test_actors.py used to call `get_broker(use_stub=True)` at module import
   5: time, which decorated the dramatiq actors against THAT StubBroker. The
   6: acceptance suite then created a DIFFERENT StubBroker in its fixture,
   7: producing `QueueNotFound: default` when calling `broker.join(...)`.
   8: 
   9: Fix: install ONE shared StubBroker at conftest IMPORT time (not via a
  10: fixture). Module-level execution here runs BEFORE any test module is
  11: imported by pytest collection — so when test_actors.py later imports
  12: `polaris_v6.queue.actors`, the @dramatiq.actor decorator binds against
  13: this StubBroker. Both test_actors.py and the acceptance suite reuse the
  14: same broker via `dramatiq.get_broker()`.
  15: 
  16: Tested: `pytest tests/v6/` runs with deterministic broker state — no
  17: QueueNotFound, no accidental Redis connection attempts.
  18: """
  19: 
  20: from __future__ import annotations
  21: 
  22: import os
  23: 
  24: import pytest
  25: 
  26: # Force StubBroker BEFORE any other test module imports `dramatiq` —
  27: # otherwise dramatiq's `get_broker()` auto-creates a default RedisBroker.
  28: os.environ.setdefault("POLARIS_V6_QUEUE_USE_STUB", "1")
  29: 
  30: # I-carney-004 P1: every create_app() call now invokes verify_app_startup()
  31: # which raises RuntimeError on missing POLARIS_JWT_SECRET / static_accounts.
  32: # Tests that mount the full app must bypass the auth substrate; individual
  33: # auth tests opt back in by `monkeypatch.delenv("POLARIS_AUTH_DISABLED")`.
  34: os.environ.setdefault("POLARIS_AUTH_DISABLED", "1")
  35: 
  36: try:
  37:     from polaris_v6.queue.broker import get_broker as _get_broker
  38: 
  39:     # Eagerly install the StubBroker. Subsequent `import dramatiq` calls
  40:     # see this broker; subsequent `@dramatiq.actor` decorations bind to it.
  41:     _SHARED_TEST_BROKER = _get_broker(use_stub=True)
  42: except ImportError:
  43:     # dramatiq isn't installed — let individual tests use pytest.importorskip
  44:     _SHARED_TEST_BROKER = None
  45: 
  46: 
  47: @pytest.fixture(autouse=True)
  48: def _isolated_run_db(tmp_path, monkeypatch):
  49:     """Isolate the v6 run DB per test (I-rdy-013).
  50: 
  51:     `run_store` reads `POLARIS_V6_RUN_DB` on every connection, so pointing it
  52:     at a fresh temp file per test prevents cross-test state from leaking. The
  53:     1-concurrent-session gate makes this mandatory: a `queued` run left behind
  54:     by an earlier test would otherwise make a later test's `POST /runs` return
  55:     409. `monkeypatch` auto-restores the env var after each test.
  56:     """

   1: """Run-status response schema.
   2: 
   3: I-arch-001a (2026-05-12): split lifecycle (operational) from pipeline_status
   4: (pipeline-A manifest verdict). Old `status` retained as computed alias for
   5: tests/v6/ backcompat — populated from lifecycle_status.
   6: 
   7: I-rdy-011 (2026-05-16): `cancel_requested` surfaced so the UI can show a
   8: cancel as in-flight in <5s, before an in-progress run reaches the next
   9: pipeline stage boundary and transitions to terminal `cancelled`.
  10: """
  11: 
  12: from __future__ import annotations
  13: 
  14: from typing import Literal
  15: 
  16: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, computed_field
  17: 
  18: LifecycleStatus = Literal[
  19:     "queued",
  20:     "in_progress",
  21:     "completed",
  22:     "cancelled",
  23:     "failed",
  24: ]
  25: 
  26: PipelineStatus = Literal[
  27:     "success",
  28:     "partial_outline_fallback",
  29:     "partial_qwen_advisory",  # legacy alias (I-modref-004 #530) — historical manifests
  30:     "partial_evaluator_advisory",
  31:     "partial_thin_corpus",
  32:     "partial_incomplete_corpus",
  33:     "partial_rule_check_warnings",
  34:     "abort_scope_rejected",
  35:     "abort_corpus_inadequate",
  36:     "abort_corpus_approval_denied",
  37:     "abort_no_verified_sections",
  38:     "abort_no_sources",
  39:     "abort_evaluator_critical",
  40:     "error_unexpected",
  41: ]
  42: 
  43: # Backcompat alias used by older code/tests (tests/v6/ asserts body['status']
  44: # and record.status). Computed from lifecycle_status by the model.
  45: RunStatus = LifecycleStatus
  46: 
  47: 
  48: class RunStatusResponse(BaseModel):
  49:     run_id: str = Field(..., description="Server-assigned UUID hex.")
  50:     lifecycle_status: LifecycleStatus = Field(
  51:         ...,
  52:         description="Operational lifecycle: queued → in_progress → completed|failed|cancelled.",
  53:     )
  54:     pipeline_status: PipelineStatus | None = Field(
  55:         default=None,
  56:         description="Pipeline-A manifest verdict. NULL until run reaches a terminal pipeline state.",
  57:     )
  58:     template: str
  59:     question: str
  60:     queued_at: str = Field(..., description="ISO8601 UTC.")
  61:     started_at: str | None = None
  62:     finished_at: str | None = None
  63:     result_json: str | None = None
  64:     error_json: str | None = None
  65:     # I-arch-001a new optional fields for UUID/slug/artifact_dir mapping.
  66:     query_slug: str | None = None
  67:     manifest_run_id: str | None = None
  68:     artifact_dir: str | None = None
  69:     cost_usd: float | None = None
  70:     decision_id: str | None = None
  71:     # I-rdy-011: True once a cancel has been requested. For a queued run the
  72:     # request is applied atomically (lifecycle_status flips to 'cancelled');
  73:     # for an in_progress run this stays True while lifecycle_status is still
  74:     # 'in_progress', until the worker observes it at a stage boundary.
  75:     cancel_requested: bool = Field(
  76:         default=False,
  77:         description="True iff cancellation has been requested for this run.",
  78:     )
  79: 
  80:     @computed_field  # serialized in JSON and readable as attr
  81:     @property
  82:     def status(self) -> LifecycleStatus:
  83:         """Deprecated alias for lifecycle_status (kept for tests/v6/ backcompat).
